\index{avdecc\+\_\+lib\+::end\+\_\+station\+\_\+imp@{avdecc\+\_\+lib\+::end\+\_\+station\+\_\+imp}!background\+\_\+read\+\_\+deduce\+\_\+next@{background\+\_\+read\+\_\+deduce\+\_\+next}}
\index{background\+\_\+read\+\_\+deduce\+\_\+next@{background\+\_\+read\+\_\+deduce\+\_\+next}!avdecc\+\_\+lib\+::end\+\_\+station\+\_\+imp@{avdecc\+\_\+lib\+::end\+\_\+station\+\_\+imp}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{background\+\_\+read\+\_\+deduce\+\_\+next(configuration\+\_\+descriptor $\ast$cd, uint16\+\_\+t desc\+\_\+type, void $\ast$frame, ssize\+\_\+t pos)}{background_read_deduce_next(configuration_descriptor *cd, uint16_t desc_type, void *frame, ssize_t pos)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}void background\+\_\+read\+\_\+deduce\+\_\+next (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf configuration\+\_\+descriptor} $\ast$}]{cd, }
\item[{uint16\+\_\+t}]{desc\+\_\+type, }
\item[{void $\ast$}]{frame, }
\item[{ssize\+\_\+t}]{read\+\_\+desc\+\_\+offset}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [private]}}\hypertarget{classavdecc__lib_1_1end__station__imp_ac9f6c6b15267ddc8bffecf2654a6f03d}{}\label{classavdecc__lib_1_1end__station__imp_ac9f6c6b15267ddc8bffecf2654a6f03d}


Deduce what else needs to be read from the rx\textquotesingle{}d frame. 

This function looks inside rx\textquotesingle{}d descriptors and deducees which descriptors need to be read in the background next. There are two lists that are maintained for reading descriptors. The m\+\_\+backbround\+\_\+read\+\_\+pending list where descriptors are queued before being sent and the m\+\_\+backbround\+\_\+read\+\_\+inflight list the contains read requests that are on \char`\"{}the wire\char`\"{}. 

end\+\_\+station\+\_\+imp.\+cpp 파일의 563 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.

The status of the End Station connection. \textquotesingle{}C\textquotesingle{} if connected. An End Station is connected after capturing an A\+DP packet with a different and unique Entity ID. \textquotesingle{}D\textquotesingle{} if disconnected. An End Station is disconnected after it fails to advertise through A\+DP for 62,000 milliseconds.

Send a R\+E\+A\+D\+\_\+\+D\+E\+S\+C\+R\+I\+P\+T\+OR command to read a descriptor from an A\+V\+D\+E\+CC Entity. Reading a descriptor can be performed by any A\+V\+D\+E\+CC Controller even when the A\+V\+D\+E\+CC Entitys locked or acquired as the act of reading the descriptor does not affect the A\+V\+D\+E\+CC Entity state.


\begin{DoxyParams}{매개변수}
{\em notification\+\_\+id} & A void pointer to the unique identifier associated with the command. \\
\hline
{\em desc\+\_\+type} & The type of the descriptor to be read by the command. \\
\hline
{\em desc\+\_\+index} & The index of the descriptor to be read by the command. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}


\hyperlink{classavdecc__lib_1_1end__station_a28ef0a87c0f86fde09e184afba1dbc56}{end\+\_\+station}를 구현.



end\+\_\+station\+\_\+imp.\+cpp 파일의 147 번째 라인에서 정의되었습니다.
